   if( true && true ) {
  const NEXTURL = 'https://fusion.inquirer.com';
  var next_trial_group = getCookie('next_trial_home_group');

  if (next_trial_group) {
    if (next_trial_group === 'beta' || (next_trial_group === 'test' && true === true)) {
      window.location.href = NEXTURL + window.location.pathname;
    }
  } else {
    randNumber = Math.random();
    var nextTrialPercentage = 20;
    if (randNumber <= 0.02*nextTrialPercentage) {
      cvalue = (Math.random()<0.5) ? "test" : "control";
    } else {
        cvalue = "excluded";
    }   
    setCookie('next_trial_home_group', cvalue, 30);
    if (cvalue == 'test' && true === true) {
      window.location.href = NEXTURL + window.location.pathname;
    }
  }

  function getCookie(name) {
		var re = new RegExp(name + "=[^;]+", "i"); //construct RE to search for target name/value pair
		if (document.cookie.match(re)) {//if cookie found
			return document.cookie.match(re)[0].split("=")[1]; //return its value
		}
	}

  function setCookie(cname, cvalue, exdays) {
    var d = new Date();
    d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays*24*60*60*1000));
    var expires = "expires="+ d.toUTCString();
    document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + ";" + expires + ";path=/;domain=inquirer.com;";
  }
}

                <div class="text-trans font-flag text-container full-width container-column">
                 <h3 class="spaced spaced-sm spaced-bottom font-bold align-left">
                  <a class="hover-unchanged-color headline-link" data-link-type="topper" data-pb-field="content.headlines.basic" data-pb-field-type="text" data-pb-placeholder="Write headline here" data-pb-url-field="canonical_url" href="/education/study-abroad-temple-arcadia-coronavirus-20210321.html">
                   The pandemic hasn’t stopped these Temple students from studying abroad
                  </a>
                 </h3>
                 <div class="byline-timestamp-container container-row align-items-center spaced spaced-bottom spaced-sm full-height">
                  <div class="byline-wrapper container-row">
                   <div class="card-byline font-semi-bold">
                    <span class="spaced spaced-right spaced-xs">
                     <a class="hover-underlined" href="https://www.inquirer.com/author/snyder_susan/">
                      <span>
                       <span class="author-name">
                        by Susan Snyder
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </a>
                    </span>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="spaced preview-text" data-pb-field="content.description.basic" data-pb-field-type="text" data-pb-placeholder="Write blurb here">
                  With campuses in Rome and Tokyo, Temple is one of few schools in the region that has resumed study abroad this semester.
                 </div>
                 <ul class="list-styled pad pad-left pad-md related-links">
                  <li class="font-bold spaced spaced-bottom spaced-sm related-url" data-rc-endpoint="v4">
                   <a class="hover-unchanged-color color-grey-ultra-dark" data-link-type="topper" href="/news/international-student-ice-lehigh-penn-state-20200804.html">
                    Local colleges pave the way for international students to start studies in their home countries, given visa restrictions
                   </a>
                  </li>
                  <li class="font-bold spaced spaced-bottom spaced-sm related-url" data-rc-endpoint="v4">
                   <a class="hover-unchanged-color color-grey-ultra-dark" data-link-type="topper" href="/education/study-abroad-villanova-dickinson-penn-coronavirus-cancel-20200609.html">
                    Colleges are canceling study abroad for the fall. What does this mean for students?
                   </a>
                  </li>
                  <li class="font-bold spaced spaced-bottom spaced-sm related-url" data-rc-endpoint="v4">
                   <a class="hover-unchanged-color color-grey-ultra-dark" data-link-type="topper" href="/education/coronavirus-arcadia-university-shuts-down-study-abroad-spring-break-20200304.html">
                    Arcadia, Penn State, Rutgers shut down all spring break study-abroad trips due to coronavirus
                   </a>
                  </li>
                 </ul>

            // We can use this to send test messages
            window.FIREBASE_MESSAGING_TOKEN = token;
            
            if (token && window.localStorage.getItem('FCM_TOKEN') !== token) {
              window.localStorage.setItem('FCM_TOKEN', token);

              var environment = window.pb_global.environment;
              var url;
              if (environment === 'dev' || environment === 'stage') {
                var url = 'https://dev.api.inquirer.com/v1/graphql/notifications';
              } else {
                var url = 'https://api.inquirer.com/v1/graphql/notifications';
              }
              
              return fetch(url, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: {
                  'Accept': 'application/json',
                  'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                  'apikey': 'LKcMPtAiPRQmXqcHpLsBW2KEnTxDYGsA',
                  'x-environment': environment
                },
                body: JSON.stringify({
                  query: "mutation($token: String!) { setToken(token: $token, platform: WEB) }",
                  variables: { token: token }
                }),
              });
            }
          }).catch(function(err) {
            console.log('Denied', err);
          });
      }); 
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Firebase initialization error:', error)
    }
  }
         </script>
        </div>
        <div class="pb-container">
        </div>
       </section>
      </div>
     </main>
    </div>
   </div>

    </script>
    <script defer="" src="https://z.moatads.com/philadelphiamediaheader375366023461/moatheader.js">

    <script>
     tp = window["tp"] || [];
    tp.push(["setAid", 'HtZYnkXBmA']);
    tp.push(["setEndpoint", 'https://api.tinypass.com/api/v3']);
    tp.push(["setUseTinypassAccounts", false ]);

    var pianoZone = 'front'.toLowerCase();
    if (document.URL.indexOf('#loaded') > -1) {
        pianoZone = 'login';
    } else if (window.PMNdataLayer[0].analytics['story_tags'] && window.PMNdataLayer[0].analytics['story_tags'].indexOf('cvfree') > -1) {
        pianoZone = 'cvfree';
    } else if (window.PMNdataLayer[0].analytics['story_tags'] && window.PMNdataLayer[0].analytics['story_tags'].indexOf('freestory') > -1) {
        pianoZone = 'freestory';
    }
    tp.push(["setZone",  pianoZone]);

    window.tp.push(['setCustomVariable', 'scrollUser', document.cookie.indexOf('scroll0=') > -1 ? 'yes' : 'no']);

    var newsletterTemplateData;
    var softstopTemplatesArray = [];
    var showTemplateArray = [];
    var eventArray = [];

    if ('front'.toLowerCase() === 'article' || 'front'.toLowerCase() === 'longform') {
        tp.push(["setContentSection", window.PMNdataLayer[0].analytics['Sub-Section']]);
        tp.push(["setContentCreated", window.PMNdataLayer[0].analytics['publishedDate'].slice(0,19)]);
    }
    tp.push(["addHandler", "showTemplate", function (templateData) {
        showTemplateArray.push(templateData);
        
        if (templateData.experienceActionId.indexOf('signup_newsletter') > -1) {
            newsletterTemplateData = templateData;
        }
        if (templateData.experienceActionId.indexOf('signup_email') > -1) {
            softstopTemplatesArray.push(templateData);
        }
    }]);
    
    tp.push(["addHandler", "customEvent", function(customEvent) {
        var clickDetail = '';
        var clickURL = customEvent.params.url || '';
        var eventNameStr = customEvent.eventName;
        var experienceActionId = customEvent.params.moduleid || '';

        if (eventNameStr.indexOf('clicked-newsletter-signup') > -1) {
            clickDetail = 'newsletter signup';
            var subSubSection = PMNdataLayer[0].analytics['Sub-Sub Section'] || '';
            subSubSection = (subSubSection.length > 0 || subSubSection !== 'No Value Set') ? subSubSection : 'null';
            var type = 'front' || PMNdataLayer[0].analytics['type'];
            var title = (type.toLowerCase() === 'article') ? 'article' : PMNdataLayer[0].analytics['title'];
            var signupSource = type + "_" + subSubSection + "_" + title + "_piano";
            
            PMNdataLayer.push({
                'event': 'piano_newsletter_registration',
                'meterAction': newsletterTemplateData.experienceActionId,
                'subscribedLists': eventNameStr.split(':')[1],
                'pianoFlag': 1,
                'signupSource': signupSource,
                'splitTestIds': (newsletterTemplateData.splitTestIds) ? newsletterTemplateData.splitTestIds : 'No Value Set',
                'displayMode': newsletterTemplateData.displayMode
            });
        }
        if (eventNameStr.indexOf('clicked-login') > -1) {
            window.services.loginService.onLoginClick();
            clickDetail = 'login';
            sessionStorage.setItem('source', 'piano_template');
        } else if (eventNameStr.indexOf('replica-login') > -1) {
            window.isReplicaLogin = true;
            clickDetail = 'login';
            window.services.loginService.onLoginClick();
        } else if (eventNameStr.indexOf('clicked-resend') > -1) {
            clickDetail = 'resend';
            window.services.loginService.resendConfirmationEmail();
        } else if (eventNameStr.indexOf('clicked-subscribe') > -1) {
            clickDetail = 'subscribe';
        } else if(eventNameStr.indexOf('clicked-activate') > -1) {
            clickDetail = 'activate';
        } else if (eventNameStr.indexOf('clicked-logout') > -1) {
            window.services.loginService.onLogoutClick();
            clickDetail = 'logout';
        } else if (eventNameStr.indexOf('clicked-back') > -1) {
            clickDetail = 'back to previous';
            var pageviews = PMNdataLayer.filter(function(obj){
                if (obj.event === 'pageview') {
                    return true;
                }
            });
            if (pageviews.length > 1) {
                // for single page apps
                var lastView = pageviews[pageviews.length - 2];
                window.location.replace(lastView.pageUrl + lastView.pagePath);
            } else {
                window.location.replace(document.referrer);
            }
        } else if (eventNameStr.indexOf('clicked-close') > -1) {
            clickDetail = 'exit';
        } else if (eventNameStr.indexOf('clicked-signup-softstop') > -1) {
            softstopTemplatesArray.forEach(function(item) {
                if(item.experienceActionId.indexOf('signup_email_softstop') > -1 && item.experienceActionId.indexOf('bottom') < 0) {
                    window.services.loginService.onLoginClick();
                    checkLockID(function(){analyticsForSignInSignUp(item, clickURL)});
                }
            });
            return;
        } else if (eventNameStr.indexOf('clicked-signup-bottom-softstop') > -1) {
            softstopTemplatesArray.forEach(function(item) {
                if(item.experienceActionId.indexOf('signup_email_softstop_bottom') > -1) {
                    window.services.loginService.onLoginClick();
                    checkLockID(function(){analyticsForSignInSignUp(item, clickURL)});
                }
            });
            return;
        } else if (eventNameStr.indexOf('clicked-signup-hardstop') > -1) {
            softstopTemplatesArray.forEach(function(item) {
                if(item.experienceActionId.indexOf('signup_email_hardstop_body') > -1) {
                    window.services.loginService.onLoginClick();
                    checkLockID(function(){analyticsForSignInSignUp(item, clickURL)});
                }
            });
            return;
        } else if (eventNameStr.indexOf('clicked-signup-bottom-hardstop') > -1) {
            softstopTemplatesArray.forEach(function(item) {
                if(item.experienceActionId.indexOf('signup_email_hardstop_bottom') > -1) {
                    window.services.loginService.onLoginClick();
                    checkLockID(function(){analyticsForSignInSignUp(item, clickURL)});
                }
            });
            return;
        }
        firePianoMeterClickEvent(clickDetail, clickURL, experienceActionId);
    }]);

    tp.push(["addHandler", "meterExpired", function(customEvent) {
        // Hide comments
        var elements = document.querySelectorAll('.pb-f-article-comments');
        for (var i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {
            elements[i].classList.add('hidden');
            elements[i].remove();
        }
    }]);

    tp.push(["addHandler", "experienceExecute", function(experienceEvent) { 
        eventArray = experienceEvent.result.events;
        var hasMeter = false;
        var splitTestIds;
        var experienceActionIdArray = [];

        for (var i = 0; i < eventArray.length; i++) {
            if (eventArray[i].eventType === 'meterActive' || eventArray[i].eventType === 'meterExpired') {
                var eventParamsObj = eventArray[i].eventParams;
                var experienceId = eventArray[i].eventExecutionContext.experienceId;
                splitTestIds = getSplitIdsForMeterStatusEvent(experienceId);

                PMNdataLayer.push({
                    "event": "meterStatus",
                    "meterStatus": 1,
                    "meterViews": eventParamsObj.totalViews,
                    "meterViewsCapped": eventParamsObj.views,
                    "meterLimit": eventParamsObj.maxViews,
                    "meterViewsLeft": eventParamsObj.viewsLeft,
                    "meterName": eventParamsObj.meterName,
                    "splitTestIds": splitTestIds
                });
                hasMeter = true;
            }

            // Get the card title of showing-template and fire piano_meter_event
            if (eventArray[i].eventType === 'showTemplate' && showTemplateArray.length > 0) {
                var experienceActionId = eventArray[i].eventModuleParams.moduleId;
                if (experienceActionIdArray.indexOf(experienceActionId) === -1) {
                    experienceActionIdArray.push(experienceActionId);
                    var index = findIndex(showTemplateArray, experienceActionId);
                    if (index > -1) {
                        pushEvent(showTemplateArray[index], eventArray[i].eventModuleParams.moduleName, 'piano_meter_event');
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        if (!hasMeter) {
            PMNdataLayer.push({
                "event": "meterStatus",
                "meterStatus": 0
            });
        }
    }]);

    // Find index for experienceActionId
    function findIndex(array, experienceActionId) {
        for (var index = 0; index < array.length; index++) {
            if (array[index].experienceActionId === experienceActionId) {
                return index;
            }
        }
        return -1;
    }

    // Get splitTestIds basing on showTemplate type object from piano. 
    function getSplitIdsForMeterStatusEvent(experienceId) {
        var splitTestIds = [];

        for (var i = 0; i < eventArray.length; i++ ) {
            var eventExecutionContextObj = eventArray[i].eventExecutionContext;
            if (eventArray[i].eventType === 'showTemplate' && eventExecutionContextObj.experienceId === experienceId) {
                if (eventExecutionContextObj.splitTests.length > 0 && splitTestIds.indexOf(eventExecutionContextObj.splitTests[0].variantId) === -1) {
                    splitTestIds.push(eventExecutionContextObj.splitTests[0].variantId);
                }
            }
        }
        if (splitTestIds.length > 0) {
            splitTestIds = JSON.stringify(splitTestIds);
        } else {
            splitTestIds = "No Value Set";
        }

        return splitTestIds;
    }

    function analyticsForSignInSignUp(templateData, clickURL) {
        // Remove any locks event before.
        window.services.loginService.lock.removeAllListeners('signup ready');
        window.services.loginService.lock.removeAllListeners('signin submit');
        window.services.loginService.lock.removeAllListeners('signup submit');

        var subSubSection = PMNdataLayer[0].analytics['Sub-Sub Section'] || '';
            subSubSection = (subSubSection.length > 0 || subSubSection !== 'No Value Set') ? subSubSection : 'null';	
        var type = 'front' || PMNdataLayer[0].analytics['type'];	
        var title = (type.toLowerCase() === 'article') ? 'article' : PMNdataLayer[0].analytics['title'];	
        var source = type + "_" + subSubSection + "_" + title + "_piano";
        var enableAuthenticatedForSignin = false;
        var enableAuthenticatedForSignup = false;

        window.services.loginService.lock.on("signup ready", function(){
            var clickDetail = "signup - " + templateData.experienceActionId;
            firePianoMeterClickEvent(clickDetail, clickURL, templateData.experienceActionId);
        });

        window.services.loginService.lock.on("signin submit", function(){
            if (!enableAuthenticatedForSignin) {
                enableAuthenticatedForSignin = true;
                window.services.loginService.lock.on("authenticated", function(authResult){
                    PMNdataLayer.push({
                        'event': 'piano_email_registration_signin',
                        'meterAction': templateData.experienceActionId,
                        'pianoFlag': 1,
                        'source': source ? source : 'No Value Set',
                        'splitTestIds': (templateData.splitTestIds) ? templateData.splitTestIds : 'No Value Set',
                        'displayMode': templateData.displayMode,
                        'authId': authResult.idTokenPayload.userId ? authResult.idTokenPayload.userId : 'No Value Set'
                    });
                });
            }
        });
        window.services.loginService.lock.on("signup submit", function(){
            if (!enableAuthenticatedForSignup) {
                enableAuthenticatedForSignup = true;
                sessionStorage.setItem('source', 'piano_registration_template');
                window.services.loginService.lock.on("authenticated", function(authResult){
                    PMNdataLayer.push({
                        'event': 'piano_email_registration_signup',
                        'meterAction': templateData.experienceActionId,
                        'pianoFlag': 1,
                        'source': source ? source : 'No Value Set',
                        'splitTestIds': (templateData.splitTestIds) ? templateData.splitTestIds : 'No Value Set',
                        'displayMode': templateData.displayMode,
                        'authId': authResult.idTokenPayload.userId ? authResult.idTokenPayload.userId : 'No Value Set'
                    });
                });
            }
        });
    }

    function firePianoMeterClickEvent(clickDetail, clickURL, experienceActionId) {
        var cardTitle = '';
        
        for (var i = 0; i < eventArray.length; i++) {
            if (eventArray[i].eventType === 'showTemplate' && eventArray[i].eventModuleParams.moduleId === experienceActionId) {
                cardTitle = eventArray[i].eventModuleParams.moduleName;
                break;
            }
        }

        var index = findIndex(showTemplateArray, experienceActionId);
        if (index > -1) {
            pushEvent(showTemplateArray[index], cardTitle, 'piano_meter_click', clickURL, clickDetail);
        }
    }

    function pushEvent(templateData, cardTitle, event, clickURL = '', clickDetail = '') {
        var activeMeters, meterLimit, meterName, meterStatus, meterViews, meterViewsCapped, meterViewsLeft;

        if (templateData.activeMeters) {
            activeMeters = JSON.parse(templateData.activeMeters)[0];
            meterLimit = activeMeters.maxViews;
            meterName = activeMeters.meterName;
            meterStatus = 1;
            meterViews = activeMeters.totalViews;
            meterViewsCapped = activeMeters.views;
            meterViewsLeft = activeMeters.viewsLeft;
        }

        var pmnObj = {
            "event" : event,
            "meterAction": templateData.experienceActionId,
            "displayMode": templateData.displayMode,
            "splitTestIds": templateData.splitTestIds || "No Value Set",
            'browserId': templateData.browserId,
            "meterStatus": meterStatus || "No Value Set",
            "meterViews": meterViews || "No Value Set",
            "meterViewsCapped": meterViewsCapped || "No Value Set",
            "meterLimit": meterLimit || "No Value Set",
            "meterViewsLeft": (meterViewsLeft || meterViewsLeft === 0) ? meterViewsLeft : "No Value Set",
            "meterName": meterName || "No Value Set",
            "cardTitle": cardTitle
        };

        switch (event) {
            case 'piano_meter_click':
                pmnObj = Object.assign(pmnObj, { "clickDetail": clickDetail, "clickURL": clickURL });
                PMNdataLayer.push(pmnObj);
                break;
            case 'piano_meter_event':
                setTimeout(function() {
                    PMNdataLayer.push(pmnObj);
                }, 0);
                break;
            default:
        }
    }

    function checkLockID(callback) {
    if (typeof callback !== 'function') throw new Error('Invalid callback handler');
    var checkLockInterval = setInterval(() => {
        if (!!window.services.loginService.lock.id)
        {
            clearInterval(checkLockInterval);
            callback();
        }
    }, 1000);
}

 <script>
  if(true || true || false || false) {
      var refreshRate = 300
var lastUserAction = 0
var hasFocus = true
var isPlayingVideo = false
var youtubes = new Array()
var goldfishes = new Array()

function reset() {
    setTimeout("lastUserAction = 0",2000)
}

function windowHasFocus() {
    hasFocus = true;
}

function windowLostFocus() {
    hasFocus = false;
}

function refresh() {
  if (lastUserAction >= refreshRate && hasFocus && !isPlayingVideo) {
    return true
  }
  return false
}

function refreshCheck() {
  if (refresh()) {
    var autoRefresh = true
    sessionStorage.setItem('autoRefresh', autoRefresh)
    window.location.reload()
    reset()
  }
}

function timedCount() {
    lastUserAction++
    refreshCheck()
    setTimeout("timedCount()",1000)
}


function onYouTubeIframeAPIReady() {
  setTimeout(function() {
    const lstIframes = document.querySelectorAll('iframe')
    if (lstIframes && lstIframes.length > 0) {
      youtubes = Array.from(lstIframes).filter(function(item) {
        if (String(item.src).indexOf('youtube.com') !== -1) {
          return item
        }
      }).map(function(item) {
        return new YT.Player(item, {
          events: {
            'onStateChange': onYoutubeStateChange,
          }
        })
      })
    }
  }, 2000)
}


function onYoutubeStateChange(event) {
  if (event.data === YT.PlayerState.PLAYING) {
    isPlayingVideo = true
  } else {
    if (detectGoldfishesPlaying() || detectYoutubesPlaying()) {
      isPlayingVideo = true
    } else {
      isPlayingVideo = false
      lastUserAction = 0
    }
  }
  window.focus()
}


function detectYoutubesPlaying() {
  var hasYoutubePlaying = false
  if (youtubes && youtubes.length > 0) {
    youtubes.forEach(function(item) {
      if (item.l.playerState === YT.PlayerState.PLAYING) {
        hasYoutubePlaying = true
      }
    })
  }
  return hasYoutubePlaying
}


function detectGoldfishVideo() {
  const videoContainers = document.querySelectorAll('.powa')
  if (videoContainers && videoContainers.length > 0) {
    videoContainers.forEach(function(item, index) {
      item.addEventListener('click', function() {
        const video = item.querySelector('video')
        onGoldfishStateChange(video)
        goldfishes[index] = video
      })
    })
  }
}


function onGoldfishStateChange(video) {
  if (video) {
    video.addEventListener('playing', function() {
      isPlayingVideo = true
    })
    video.addEventListener('pause', function() {
      if (detectGoldfishesPlaying() || detectYoutubesPlaying()) {
        isPlayingVideo = true
      } else {
        isPlayingVideo = false
        lastUserAction = 0
      }
    })
  }
}


function detectGoldfishesPlaying() {
  var isHasGoldfishPlaying = false
  if (goldfishes && goldfishes.length > 0) {
    goldfishes.forEach(function(item) {
      if (!item.paused) {
        isHasGoldfishPlaying = true
      }
    })
  }
  return isHasGoldfishPlaying
}

window.addEventListener("focus", windowHasFocus, false);
window.addEventListener("blur", windowLostFocus, false);
window.addEventListener('click', reset, false)
window.addEventListener('mousemove', reset, false)
window.addEventListener('keypress', reset, false)
window.addEventListener('scroll', reset, false)

detectGoldfishVideo()
timedCount()

    }
 </script>
